  `dsID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `fID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `fvID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `uID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,

  `bID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
